a art

英音 ə; eɪ 美音 ə; eɪ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [a一般用于以辅音音素开始的词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (非特指的) 一 (个)：

a university
一所大学

an honest man
一个老实人

  1. 高义频： (一类事物中的) 任何一个 (any)：

A square has four sides.
正方形有四条边。

  1. 高义频： 一 (one)：

Rome was not built in a day.
罗马不是一天建成的。

  1. 高义频： 每一 (each)：

twenty dollars a week
每周20美元

three times a day
一日三次

  1. 高义频： 某一 (a certain，用于专有名词特别是人名前)：

Brian is gifted in writing music; he is very likely to be a Beethoven.
布莱恩有作曲天赋，他很有可能成为又一个贝多芬。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

Each of my cafes will have a different theme and an unique style.

答案 an → a
题目

As the kid,I love to watch cartoons.

答案 the → a
题目

It takes them about a hour and a half to go to work every day.

答案 第一个a → an / one
题目

I can't tell you ____ way to the Wilsons' because we don't have ____ Wilson here in the village.

答案 the; a
题目

The paper is due next month, and I am working seven days ____ week, often long into ____ night.
A.a; the

答案 a; the

abandon vt

英音 ə'bændən 美音 ə'bændən

词频 3 | 口语 0 | 书面 1 | 阅读 3

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 放弃
    to stop doing or having sth：

abandoned,hope
Rescuers had abandoned all hope of finding any more survivors.
营救人员对找到更多生还者已不抱任何希望。

These plans were abandoned because of financial problems.
因为经济方面的原因，这些计划被终止了。

  1. 高义频： 遗弃
    to leave sb, especially sb you're responsible for：

How could she abandon her own child?
她怎么能抛弃自己的孩子呢？

People find all sorts of excuses for abandoning an animal.
人们为遗弃动物找出各种借口。

  1. 高义频： 离弃
    to leave a place, vehicle etc., especially because it is impossible or dangerous to stay (leave)：

Snow forced many drivers to abandon their vehicles.
雪迫使许多司机弃车而行。

Fearing further attacks, most of the population had abandoned the city.
由于害怕遭受更多的袭击，大多数市民逃离了这座城市。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

abandoned /ə'bændənd/ adj

A shared bike is left abandoned at a bus stop.
一辆共享单车被遗弃在公交车站。

真题解析

[null]

ability n

英音 ə'bɪləti 美音 ə'bɪləti

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [U] 能力
    the fact of being able to do sth： 反义词 inability

  • ability to do sth:

The ability to laugh and smile is actually something we are born with.
笑与微笑实际上是我们与生俱来的能力。

  1. 高义频： [C] & [U] 才能；才识；技能
    a level of skill at doing sth：

develop an ability
培养技能

musical,natural,ability
musical / natural ability
音乐才能/天赋

of all abilities
Students of all abilities will get together and study for two weeks.
各种水平的学生将聚集在一起学习两个星期。

固定搭配

  • to the best of one's ability

  1. 尽最大努力：

I try to do my job to the best of my ability.
我尽全力做好我的工作。

able adj

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 能：
    反义词 unable

  • (be) able to do sth:

Looking back, I feel I wouldn’t be able to ride a bike had I lost heart.
回想起来，我觉得如果当初自己失去信心，就不能学会骑自行车了。

Being able to make small talk is a very useful skill in relating with other people.
能与人闲谈是和他人打交道的非常实用的技能。

  1. 低义频： 能干的；有能力的：

Even the most able students found the test difficult.
连能力最强的学生都觉得这次测验很难。

about prep

英音 əˈbaʊt 美音 əˈbaʊt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 关于：

The passage is about the writer's childhood.
这篇文章讲述的是作者的童年。

I want to talk to you about changing my major.
我想和你谈谈我换专业的事。

  1. 低义频： 在...周围；到处 (AmE around, BrE round)：

I planted bamboo about my house.
我在房子四周栽种了竹子。

After dinner I wandered alone about the town.
饭后我一个人在城里四处逛了逛。

  1. 高义频： 目的是；为了:

all about
Tiger parenting is all about raising independent,creative and brave kids.
“虎妈家教”的目的是培养独立、有创造力和勇敢的孩子。

固定搭配

  • What / How about ...?

  1. …怎么样？

What / How about the weather in Qinghai Province?
青海省的天气如何？

What / How about meeting at the nearby restaurant?
在附近的饭店见面怎么样？

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

Modern equipment and no smoking are two of the things I like ____ working here.

答案 about

 

about adv

英音 əˈbaʊt 美音 əˈbaʊt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 大约；左右：

It’s about 10 minutes’ walk.
步行大约需要10分钟。

  1. 高义频： 在 / 向周围；四处：

Look about and tell me what you see.
向四周看看，告诉我你看到了什么。

  1. 高义频： 将近；差不多：

Supper is about ready.
晚饭快好了。

My stomach is about full.
我的肚子差不多饱了。

固定搭配

  • be about to do sth

  1. 正要 / 准备做某事：

I was about to turn off my computer when I received an email.
我正准备关电脑,这时收到了一封电子邮件。

be about to常与when连用，表示“刚要…突然…”。

[null]

题目

Tom was about to close the window ____ his attention was caught by a bird.

above prep

英音 əˈbʌv 美音 əˈbʌv

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 在...上方：
    反义词 below

We were flying above the clouds.
我们在云层上面飞行。

辨析 above, on, over

三者都含有“在…上”之意。

  1. 高义频： (数量 / 程度 / 地位等) 大于；超出；高于：

above freezing
The temperature was only a few degrees above freezing.
气温仅为零上几度。

He values health above wealth.
他重视健康甚于财富。

above and beyond the call of duty
above and beyond the call of duty (=more than the duty)
超越职责要求

固定搭配

  • above all

  1. 最重要的是；尤其：

I’d like to buy a house — modern, comfortable, and above all in a quiet neighborhood.
我要买一座房子，要现代、要舒适，最重要的是周围要安静。

absence n

英音 ˈæbsəns 美音 ˈæbsəns

词频 2 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 | 阅读 2

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [C] & [U] 缺席；不在：

absence from
He was eager to be back after more than a week’s absence from school.
他一个多星期没有去学校，急切地想回去。

  1. 高义频： [U] 缺乏：

absence of mind
Her absence of mind during driving nearly caused an accident.
她驾车时心不在焉，差点造成事故。

固定搭配

  • in / during sb’s absence

  1. 在某人不在时：

In his absence I looked to see what was on his desk.
趁他不在时，我看了看他桌上有什么东西。

  • in the absence of

  1. 在缺乏…的情况下：

In the absence of gray wolves, the deer population grew quickly.
没有了灰狼，鹿的数量迅速增长

absolutely adv

英音 'æbsəlu:tli 美音 'æbsəlu:tli

词频 3 | 口语 3 | 书面 1 | 阅读 1

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 完全地；绝对地 (quite)：

He made his reasons for resigning absolutely clear.
他把辞职的理由讲得一清二楚。

— People don’t care enough about the environment.
人们对环境关心不够。

— I think you’re absolutely right.
我认为你说的完全正确。

  1. 高义频： [用于强调] 确实：

absolutely nothing
When I’m reading a book, absolutely nothing can get my attention.
当我读书时，其他任何东西都不能引起我的注意。

absolutely no
— You’re sure there’s absolutely no hot water?
你确定确实没有热水吗？

— No, none.
是的，没有。

固定搭配

  • Absolutely!

  1. 正是；当然：

— They could have told us, couldn't they?
他们本来可以告诉我们的，不是吗？

— Absolutely!
正是！

  • Absolutely not!

  1. 绝对不行；当然不：

— Do you let your kids travel alone at night?
你让自己的孩子们晚上单独外出吗？

— Absolutely not!
当然不!

absorb vt 重难点词汇

英音 əbˈsɔːb 美音 əbˈsɔːrb

词频 3 | 口语 0 | 书面 1 | 阅读 3

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 吸收
    to take in and hold sth (a liquid, heat, etc.)：

A transparent object doesn’t absorb light.
透明的物体不吸收光。

One hectare of forest can absorb 23 tons of carbon dioxide per year
一公顷森林每年可以吸收23吨二氧化碳。

  1. 低义频： 吸纳
    to take sth into sth larger, so that it becomes part of it：

Service work absorbed a great number of women who arrived in the cities from the country.
服务业吸纳了很多从农村来到城市的妇女。

  1. 高义频： 理解；掌握
    to take sth into the mind and understand it(take in)：

absorb new knowledge / information
掌握新知识/新信息

I’ve just been so busy studying and trying to absorb all the new things around me.
我一直忙于学习，并试图理解身边所有的新事物。

  1. 低义频： 吸引；使专心
    to interest sb so much that they don’t pay attention to other things：

This work has absorbed him for years.
多年来，他一直专注于这项工作。

  1. 低义频： 缓冲：

Well-designed sports shoes should absorb the impact on your feet.
设计精良的运动鞋可以缓解脚部受到的冲击。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

absorbed /əb'sɔːbd/ adj

When something did interest me, I could become absorbed.
当某件事确实让我感兴趣时，我就能够全神贯注。

( be ) absorbed in:
( be ) absorbed in:

When deeply absorbed in work, he always forgets all about eating or sleeping.
他专注工作时，总是废寝忘食。

accept v 重难点词汇

英音 ək'sept 美音 əkˈsept

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 接受：

accept sb’s advice / suggestion
accept sb’s advice / suggestion
接受某人的建议

accept a gift / an invitation
accept a gift / an invitation
接受礼物/邀请

They offered me a job and I accepted.
他们给我提供一份工作，我接受了。

It’s generally accepted that
It’s generally accepted that people are motivated by success.
人们普遍认为成功催人奋进。

accept that
While I accept that he is not perfect, I do actually like the person.
我承认他不够完美，但我的确喜欢这个人。

辨析 accept, receive

receive 表示客观上收到，accept 表示主观上愿意接受。

She received a gift from him, but did not accept it.
她收到了他的礼物，但没有接受。

  1. 高义频： 忍受；承受
    to continue in a difficult situation without complaining, because you can’t change it：

accept,the,fact,that
We have to accept ( the fact ) that this is not a perfect world.
我们必须接受这样的现实，这不是个完美的世界。

In my opinion, people need to learn to accept the reality and keep on trying.
在我看来，人必须学会接受现实，并不断努力。

  1. 高义频： 接纳
    to allow sb to join a group, etc.：

The college I applied to has accepted me.
我申请的学院已经录取我了。

accepted as
I hope I will be accepted as a member of your summer camp.
我希望能成为你们夏令营中的一员。

  1. 高义频： 承担 (责任 / 指责)
    to admit that you’re responsible or to blame for sth：

accept the blame for
I refuse to accept the blame for something that was someone else’s fault.
我拒绝为别人的过错承担责任。

accept the responsibility for
It seems that most people don’t want to accept the responsibility for having made a mistake.
似乎大多数人不想对已犯的错误负责。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

答案 accepted
题目

答案 accepted

  1. 高义频： 可接受的；令人满意的：
    反义词 unacceptable

acceptable to
an agreement which is acceptable to both sides
双方都可接受的协议

socially acceptable
It is not socially acceptable for parents to leave children unattended at that age.
父母丢下那个年纪的孩子不照看，社会是不接受这种做法的。

access n 重难点词汇

英音 ˈækses 美音 ˈækses

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 3

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 通道；入口
    a way of reaching or entering a place：

access to
Fallen rocks cut off the only access to the village.
坠石挡住了通往村子的唯一道路。

gained access
The police gained access through a broken window.
警察从一扇破窗中钻了进去。

  1. 高义频： 使用 / 接近…的权利或机会
    the opportunity or right to use sth or to see sb / sth：

Each room comes with its own bathroom and Internet access.
每个房间都有浴室，都能上网。

have no access to
Across the world, 1.1 billion people have no access to clean drinking water.
全世界有11亿人喝不到干净的饮用水。

instant access to
This site gives you instant access to a wide range of information on studying and living in the UK.
这个网站让你瞬间即可查到关于在英国学习和居住的各种各样的信息。

have easy access to
One reason for her preference for city life is that she can have easy access to places like shops and restaurants.
她喜欢城市生活的一个原因是去哪儿都很方便，比如去商店和餐馆。

access ≠ way, access作为名词，其含义中包含了某种动作。

accident n

英音 ˈæksɪdənt 美音 ˈæksɪdənt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 事故：

avoid / meet / cause an accident
避免/遇到/造成事故

in a car accident
He was killed in a car accident.
他死于车祸。

had_1,accident
Ken had an accident at work and had to go to hospital.
肯在工作中出了事故，不得不去医院。

  1. 低义频： 偶然的事；意外的事
    sth that happens unexpectedly and is not planned in advance：

The discovery was a happy accident.
这个发现是机缘巧合。

固定搭配

  • by accident

  1. 偶然地；意外地
    反义词 on purpose

Yesterday when I was wandering on the pavement near a park, I met an old neighbour by accident.
昨天当我正在公园附近的人行道上闲逛时，偶然遇到了一位从前的邻居。

辨析 accident, incident, event

三者都含有“事件”之意。

account n 重难点词汇

英音 ə'kaʊnt 美音 əˈkaʊnt

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 3

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [常用复数] 账；账目：

an account book
账本；账簿

He takes care of the business and his wife keeps the accounts.
他打理生意，他太太则负责记账。

  1. 高义频： 账户；账号：

open / close an account
open / close an account
开/销户

have an account at / with a bank
have an account at / with a bank
在银行开户

create an e-mail account
创建电子邮件账户

the WeChat offical / public account
微信公众号

a bank account
My father helped me set up a bank account.
我爸爸帮我开了个银行账户。

  1. 低义频： 叙述；报道；描写：

eye-witness account of
an eye-witness account of a murder
目击者对一起谋杀的描述

gives an account of
While this book tells the stories of famous people in history, it also gives an account of the lives of lesserknown individuals.
这本书在讲述历史名人的故事的同时，还讲述不太出名的人的生活。

固定搭配

  • on account of

  1. 因为；由于 (because of)：

She was absent from school on account of illness.
她因病没有去学校。

  • on no account

  1. 决不；绝对不：

The professor warned the students that on no account should they use mobile phones in his class.
教授警告学生，在他的课上绝对不能玩手机。

on no account置于句首，其所在的句子要用倒装语序。

  • take account of / take ... into account

  1. 考虑到；把…考虑进去：

The company takes account of environmental issues wherever possible.
只要有可能，这家公司都会考虑到环境问题。

One must take the audience into account when making speeches.
人们在演讲时必须要考虑听众。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

I ____ (开了个银行账户) after I made $1,000 by doing a part-time job during the summer vacation.

答案 opened/set up a bank account

 

account v 重难点词汇

英音 ə'kaʊnt 美音 əˈkaʊnt

词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 | 阅读 3

英文释义

[null]

固定搭配

  • account for

  1. 高义频： (数量、比例上) 占：

It is said that body language accounts for 55 percent of a first impression while what you say just 7 percent.
据说肢体语言在第一印象中占55%，而你所说的话仅占7%。

  1. 高义频： 是...的原因；解释 / 说明(explain)：

The application of new technologies and wide appeal of movie stars could account for the increase of the box-office income.
新技术的应用和影星们的广泛号召力可能是票房收入增加的原因。

Can you account for your behaviour on that night?
你能解释一下你那天晚上的行为吗？

The poor weather may have accounted for the small crowd.
天气不好可能是人来得少的原因。

achieve v 重难点词汇

英音 əˈtʃiːv 美音 əˈtʃiːv

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 3

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (凭借努力) 达到 (目标、地位、标准)
    to succeed in reaching a particular goal, status or standard, especially after much effort (attain)：

achieve success / progress
achieve success / progress
取得成功 / 进步

Happiness is achieved through hard work.
幸福是奋斗出来的。

achieve my,goals
I used to try effective methods to achieve my academic goals.
为实现自己的学习目标，我曾尝试过一些有效的方法。

  1. 低义频： 完成
    to succeed in doing sth or causing sth to happen (accomplish)：

No one can achieve anything without effort.
没有人能够不努力就有所成就。

He achieved what he had thought impossible.
他做成了自己以为不可能的事。

  1. 低义频： 获得成功
    to be successful：

He is an excellent lawyer with a good brain and a determination to achieve.
他是位优秀的律师，具有好的头脑和取得成功的决心。

France is Europe’s third largest country and faces the United Kingdom across the English Channel.
法国是欧洲第三大国家，隔英吉利海峡与英国相望。

Do you think this shirt is too tight across the shoulders?

辨析 across , through

  1. 高义频： 在…另一边；在…对面：

Nelson Mandela is respected and admired across the world.

act v 重难点词汇

英音 ækt 美音 ækt

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 行动；做事：

Think twice before you act.
三思而后行。

  1. 高义频： 举止；表现
    to behave in a particular way (behave)：

Those who have more money than sense may sometimes act foolishly.
有钱但缺乏理智的人有时可能举止愚蠢。

act as if
I was in great pain at that moment, but I tried to act as if nothing had happened.
那一刻我感到非常疼痛，但我尽力表现得好像什么也没发生过似的。

  1. 高义频： 假装
    to pretend to have feelings, qualities, etc. that are different from your true ones：

act the fool
Don’t act the fool!
别装傻！

  1. 高义频： 演 (戏)；扮演 (角色)：

He had always wanted to act in films, so he moved to Hollywood.
他一直想演电影，于是搬到了好莱坞。

Who’s acting (the part of) Hamlet?
谁来扮演哈姆雷特（的角色）？

固定搭配

  • act as

  1. 担任；充当；起…作用：

经过训练的狗可以充当盲人的向导。

  • act on

  1. 高义频： 按照...行事(act upon)：

Why didn’t you act on her suggestion?
你为什么不按照她的建议来做呢？

  1. 高义频： 对... 起作用 / 有影响：

Alcohol acts quickly on the brain.
酒精对大脑迅速产生影响。

  • act out

  1. 把…表演出来；将…付诸行动；充当：

act out a story / dialogue
把故事/对话表演出来

act out a theory
把理论付诸实践

add v

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 增添；增加：

If the tea is too strong, add some more water.

粗话、辱骂和指责只会火上浇油。

  1. 高义频： vi & vt (使) 相加：

Add,7,and,5,together

7加5等于12。

  1. 高义频： 补充说：

“And don’t be late,” she added.
“别迟到了，”她补充道。

The President agreed, adding that he hoped for a peaceful solution.
总统表示赞同，补充说他希望一个和平的解决方法。

固定搭配

  • add to

  1. 增加：

Colorful umbrellas add to a lively atmosphere in the summer streets.
各种颜色的伞给夏日街头平添了活泼的气氛。

  • add up

  1. 把…加起来；合计：

Add up your score and see how many points you get.
把你的分数加起来，看看你得多少分。

  • add up to

  1. 合计达；结果是：

His debts added up to $5,000.
他的欠债合计达到5000美元。

Remember: little steps add up to big dreams.
记住：小进步成就大梦想。

You’ll quickly adjust yourself to student life.
你将很快适应学生生活。

Over the years, we all learned to adjust and to become more comfortable with each other.
几年来，我们都学会了适应，学会了彼此宽容。

在日常英语中常用get used to，而不用adjust。

admit v 重难点词汇

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 容许...进入
    to allow sb / sth to enter a place：

A hole in the top of the roof admitted the light.
房顶的小洞能透进光线。

admitted to / into
Only ticket-holders will be admitted to / into the stadium.
持票者方可进入体育场。

  1. 低义频： 接纳；招收
    to allow sb to become a member of a club, a school, etc.：

be admiitted to

我很有可能会被我梦想的大学录取。

The table-tennis team of our school is admitting new players.
我们学校的乒乓球队正在招收新队员。

  1. 高义频： 承认
    to agree, often unwillingly, that sth is true：

“I can’t sing at all,” he freely / openly / frankly admitted.
“我不会唱歌，”他坦率 / 公开 / 坦白承认说。

admit,to_2
We should have the courage to admit (to) our mistakes.
我们应当有勇气承认错误。

admit,to_2,being
I had to admit (to) being nervous about the test.
我不得不承认对这次考试感到紧张。

I don't really like the author, although I have to admit his books are very exciting.
尽管我不太喜欢这位作者，但不得不承认他的书还是很激动人心。

  1. 高义频： 供认
    to say that you have done sth wrong or illegal：

admit,to_2
He refused to admit (to) the other charges.
他拒不承认其他指控。

admitted ( to ) having,stealing
She admitted ( to ) having stolen / stealing the car.
她供认偷了那辆车。

advice n

英音 əd'vaɪs 美音 əd'vaɪs

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 忠告；建议：

a piece of advice
a piece of advice
一条建议

ask / seek sb’s advice / ask sb for advice
ask / seek sb’s advice / ask sb for advice
征求某人的意见

accept / follow / take sb’s advice
accept / follow / take sb’s advice
接受某人的意见

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

[null]

advise v 重难点词汇

英音 əd'vaɪz 美音 əd'vaɪz

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 劝告；建议：

  • advise sb to do sth:

I advised them to take Bus No. 20, which could take them there directly.
我建议他们乘坐20路公交车，这样他们就能直达那里。

You are advised to book in advance.
建议您提前预订。

  • advise doing sth:

They advised putting off the meeting till next week.
他们建议把会议推迟到下星期。

  • advise (sb) + that … (should) do sth:

The doctor advised Vera strongly that she (should) take a holiday.
医生强烈建议维拉休假。

It is strongly advised that
It is strongly advised that the contracts be read through thoroughly.
强烈建议把合同仔细看一遍。

  • advise (sb) on sth:

She advised the government on environmental issues.
她就环境问题给政府提建议。

It’s easy for you to advise, but difficult to take advice from others.
劝告别人容易，接受别人的劝告就难了。

辨析 advise, suggest

表示“建议”时，二者意义十分接近。但用法不尽相同。

  1. 低义频： [正式用语] 通知
    to officially tell sb sth：

  • advise sb (of sth):

Please advise us of any changes in your personal details.
你的个人资料如有变化，敬请告知。

  • advise sb + that/wh- 从句:

You’ll have about one hour to explore the area, and your tour guide will advise you what time you should be back.
你们将有约一小时的时间在这一区域考察，之后导游会通知你们几点返回。

I regret to advise you that the course is now full.
很遗憾地通知你，这门课程现在已满额。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

afforded,view

  • (be) afraid to do sth:

She is afraid to be here alone.
她不敢单独待在这里。

  1. 高义频： 担心的；忧虑的：

  • (be) afraid+(that)从句:

again adv

英音 ə'ɡen, ə'ɡeɪn 美音 ə'ɡen, ə'ɡeɪn

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 又；再：

If you fail the first time, try again.
如果第一次失败了，再试一次。

  1. 高义频： 而且；另外：

Again, spending too long at the computer results in painful wrists and fingers.
另外，长时间使用电脑还会导致手腕和手指疼痛。

固定搭配

  • again and again

  1. 再三地；反复地：

Again and again I warned him of the danger.
我一再警告他有危险。

  • then / there again

  1. 不过；另一方面：

Parents feel that it is difficult to live with teenagers. Then again, teenagers have similar feelings about their parents.
父母们觉得很难与青少年一起生活。不过，青少年对父母也有相似的感受。

[null]

against prep

英音 ə'ɡenst, ə'ɡeɪnst 美音 ə'ɡenst, ə'ɡeɪnst

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 反对：

Personally, I’m against the measure of paying students to learn.
就我个人而言，我反对用金钱鼓励学生学习的做法。

  1. 高义频： 违背；逆：

against one’s wishes / will
against one’s wishes / will
违背某人的意愿

against the law
This was against the law (= illegal).
这是违法的。

The ship is sailing against the wind.
船正在逆风航行。

  1. 高义频： 和...比赛、对抗等：

We’ll be competing against some of the best companies in Europe.
我们要和一些一流的欧洲公司竞争。

  1. 低义频： 倚靠；向着；对着：

He leaned against the door.
他倚着门。

The rain beat against the windows.
雨打在窗户上。

  1. 低义频： 防备；以备：

Squirrels store up food against the winter.
松鼠贮存食物以备过冬。

  1. 低义频： 以...为背景；衬托：

The picture looks good against the white wall.
在白墙的衬托下这幅画很好看。

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 年龄：

be of the same age
同龄

你多大了？

At the age of five / At age five, Mozart started writing classical music.
莫扎特五岁时开始创作古典音乐。

for your age
You look really young for your age.
您看上去要比您的实际年龄小。

  1. 高义频： 很长时间：

for ages
I haven’t seen you for ages.
我很长时间没看见你了。

  1. 高义频： 世纪；年代：

the Middle Ages / the Stone Age

中世纪/石器时代

固定搭配

  • under age

  1. 未到法定年龄

Every culture has developed a formal way to greet strangers, to show them we are not aggressive.

ago adv

英音 ə'ɡəʊ 美音 ə'ɡoʊ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 以前：

a,minute,moment,ago
a minute / moment ago
刚才

a little / short while ago
不久前

long, long ago
很久很久以前

I last saw him a few months ago.
我上次见到他是在几个月以前。

辨析 ago, before

二者都可作副词，表示“(某段时间) 以前”。 ago 表示从现在算起某段时间以前，before 表示从过去的某个时候算起某段时间以前。ago 常与一般过去时连用，before 常与过去完成时连用。

I don’t know where he is, but he was here a minute ago.
我不知道他现在在哪儿，但是刚才他在这儿。

I called him up yesterday, but his wife told me that he had left for Wuhan three days before.
我昨天给他打过电话，但他妻子说他三天前去武汉了。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

agree v 重难点词汇

英音 ə'ɡriː 美音 ə'ɡriː

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [不用于进行时]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (意见、观点等) 一致
    to have the same opinion as sb/sth： 反义词 disagree

— The service in the restaurant is terrible.
这家餐馆的服务真差劲。

couldn’t agree more,quite agree
— I couldn’t agree more / I quite agree.
我完全赞同。

It is,agreed that
It is generally agreed that Beijing has a traffic problem.
人们普遍认为北京的交通有问题。

agree on
Li Jiang and Su Hua don't agree on what to wear when greeting the British students.
李江和苏华在穿什么衣服去迎接英国学生的问题上意见不一。

agree on主要指双方通过协商而就某事取得一致意见或达成协议。

  1. 高义频： 同意；赞同
    to say yes to sth： 反义词 refuse

agreed to
I've agreed to go with Alice to buy some clothes.
我已经答应和爱丽丝去买衣服。

agrees to
Make sure each group member understands and agrees to the task given to him or her.
确保每个小组成员都明白并且同意派给他或她的任务。

agree to后面常接表示“提议”、“办法”、“计划”或“安排”等的词作宾语。

固定搭配

  • agree with

  1. 高义频： 同意；赞同：

agree with one’s idea / opinion
赞同某人的想法/意见

I quite agree with him on the sports.
我非常同意他在运动方面的观点。

agree with表示“同意”、“赞同”时，后常接人或表示“意见”、“看法”的词作宾语。

  1. 高义频： 与...相符；与...一致
    to be the same as sth：

His words do not agree with his actions.
他言行不一致。

  1. 高义频： [常用于否定句] (食物等) 适合
    (of food, etc.) be suitable for sb：

Too much meat doesn’t agree with her.
她不宜吃太多肉。

派生词汇

agreeable /ə'ɡriːəbl/ adj

真题解析

题目

You look well. The air and the sea foods in Sanya must agree ____ you, I suppose.

答案 with
题目

答案 on

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 同意；(意见) 一致
    反义词 disagreement：

in agreement
We are in agreement about the price.
关于价格我们意见一致。

  1. 高义频： 协定；协议：

sign an agreement
签订协议

arrive at,come to,reach an agreement,with
arrive at / come to / reach an agreement ( with)
(与…)达成协议

hold to / keep an agreement
遵守协议

an agreement, to
They had an agreement never to talk about work at home.
他们约定在家中绝不谈工作。

air n

英音 eə(r) 美音 er

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 空气；天空；空中：

air conditioning / conditioners
air conditioning / conditioners
空调系统/空调机

in the air
Birds are flying high up in the air.
鸟儿在高空中飞翔。

by air
It saves a great deal of time to travel by air.
乘飞机出行能节省很多时间。

  1. 低义频： 神态；样子：

air of
The dog hardly ate anything and had such an air of sadness.
这条狗没怎么吃东西，一副很忧郁的样子。

固定搭配

  • in the air

  1. (某种情绪) 弥漫在空气中；即将发生：

There was a sense of excitement in the air.
到处洋溢着一种激动的气氛。

Change is in the air.
变革迫在眉睫。

  • on / off (the) air

  1. 正在/停止广播：

We’ll be on air in three minutes.
我们三分钟后开始广播。

alive adj

英音 ə'laɪv 美音 ə'laɪv

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [不用于名词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 活着的【反:dead】；仍存在的：

Who is the greatest man alive?
谁是当今最伟大的人？

keep,alive
Relatives of the missing sailors are struggling to keep their hopes alive.
失踪船员的亲属们正努力不让希望破灭。

Not until two days after the earthquake did she find her mother alive.
地震发生两天后她才发现她母亲还活着。

辨析 living, alive

二者均可用作形容词，有“活着的”、“在世的”之意，但用法不尽相同。

  1. 低义频： 有活力的：

alive with
Edward was alive with happiness.
爱德华高兴得眉飞色舞。

alive 可作表语、补语或后置定语；无比较级和最高级。

固定搭配

  • come alive

  1. 高义频： 变得有趣；生动起来(come to life)：

The discussion came alive when an interesting topic was brought in.
当引入一个有趣的话题时，讨论活跃了起来。

  1. 高义频： 精神起来；活泼起来：

She came alive as she talked about her job.
她一谈到自己的工作就来精神了。

  1. 低义频： 热闹起来；变得繁忙(come to life)：

The fishing villages come alive in spring.
渔村在春季变得繁忙起来。

派生词汇

[null]

all adv 重难点词汇

英音 ɔːl 美音 ɔːl

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 完全地；十分：

My hands are all wet.
我的手全湿了。

She was dressed all in white.
她穿了一身白。

固定搭配

  • all along

  1. [非正式用语] 一直；始终：

You’ve been very nice to me all along.
你一直待我很好。

I know that all along.
那件事我自始至终都知道。

  • all but

  1. 几乎；差不多(almost)：

The party was all but over when we arrived.
我们到达时，聚会已近尾声。

  • all too

  1. [用于表示不好的情形] 极；甚：

All too often, people buy a pen based only on looks.
人们买笔时往往都只看外表。

真题解析

[null]

all pron 重难点词汇

英音 ɔːl 美音 ɔːl

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 全部；全体：

All for one, one for all.
人人为我，我为人人。

All of them enjoyed themselves.
他们都玩得很愉快。

  1. 高义频： 唯一；一切：

All (that) I need is peace and quiet.
我需要的是安宁与平静。

All is not gold that glitters.
闪光的未必都是金子。

固定搭配

  • all in all

  1. 总而言之 (altogether)：

All in all her mother and I are very happy with her progress.
总而言之，看到她的进步我和她妈妈都很高兴。

  • in all

  1. 总共 (altogether)：

How many people were there in all at the party?
出席聚会的共有多少人？

  • not ... at all

  1. 根本不；一点也不：

The ﬁlm was not interesting at all.
电影一点儿也没意思。

  • not at all

  1. [客套语] 不客气：

— It’s so kind of you and your parents.
非常感谢您和您的父母。

— Not at all.
不客气。

allow v 重难点词汇

英音 ə'laʊ 美音 ə'laʊ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 允许；准许(permit):

  • allow sb / sth to do sth:

Her parents wouldn’t allow her to go to the party, but she still hopes to.
她父母不准她去参加聚会，但她还是想去。

He allowed his mind to wander.
他任由思绪蔓延。

  • allow sb sth:

My father allows himself three cigarettes a day.
我爸爸给自己规定一天吸三根烟。

You're allowed an hour to complete the test.
给你们一个小时的时间来完成测验。

is not allowed
Smoking is not allowed in the hall.
大厅内不许抽烟。

  1. 高义频： 使...有可能
    to make sth possible (permit)：

  • allow sb / sth to do sth:

The click of a button allows people miles apart to talk or see each other without even leaving their homes.
点击一个按钮能使相距数英里的人甚至足不出户也能交谈或看见彼此。

Exploration allows minerals and other potential resources to be found.
探索让我们发现矿产和其他潜在的资源。

  • allow sb sth:

Bicycles allow people the freedom to move about that cars just can’t provide.
自行车能让人随意地四处走动，而汽车不能。

  • allow for:

The new system will allow for more efficient use of resources.
新系统将使资源得到更有效的利用。

  1. 高义频： 留出；给出 (时间、金钱、食物等)：
    to provide money, time, etc. for sb / sth：

allow,for
Buy children’s shoes big enough to allow room for growth.
孩子的鞋要买得大些，以给脚的生长留出空间。

Have you allowed yourself enough time to get to the airport?
你已留出足够的时间去机场了吗？

固定搭配

  • allow for

  1. 考虑到；顾及：

Allowing for the bad weather, we should set off right now.
考虑到天气不好，我们应该马上出发。

Has everything been allowed for in your plan?
你的计划是否把各种情况都考虑进去了？

派生词汇

allowable /ə'laʊəbl/ adj

真题解析

题目

As Jack left his membership card at home, he wasn’t allowed ____(go) into the sports club.

答案 to go
题目

The writing point of the pen should allow the ink ____ (flow) evenly (均匀地) while the pen remains in touch with the paper.

答案 to flow
题目

— Can I smoke here? — Sorry. We don’t allow ____ (smoke) here.

答案 smoking

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 限额；限量； 津贴；补贴；零用钱：

出差补助

We had to earn our allowance by doing chores around the house.
我们只好靠在家里做杂活来挣零用钱。

  • make allowance(s) for

  1. 考虑到；顾及；体谅：

Making allowances for his poor health, his boss allowed him to work six hours a day instead of eight.
老板体谅他身体不好，让他每天工作六小时而不是八小时。

alone adj

英音 ə'ləʊn 美音 ə'loʊn

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [不用于名词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 单独的；独自的：

Better be alone than in bad company.
交损友不如无友。

It’s terrible to find oneself alone in such a place.
发现独自一人在那样一个地方真可怕。

not alone in
Believe me; you’re not alone in feeling sad.
相信我，并不只是你一个人感到难过。

  1. 高义频： 孤独的；寂寞的：

felt so alone
The old man cried like a child because he felt so alone.
老人感到很孤独，像小孩子一样哭了起来。

  1. 高义频： 仅仅；只：

In the United States alone, over 100 million cellphones are thrown away each year
仅在美国，每年就有超过1亿部手机被扔掉。

固定搭配

  • leave / let sb alone

  1. 不打扰某人；不管某人：

Why don’t you just mind your own business and leave me alone?
为什么你就不能少管闲事不打扰我？

  • leave / let sth alone

  1. 不碰某物：

Leave the cakes alone. They’re for the guests.
别动那些蛋糕，那是给客人吃的。

along adv

英音 ə'lɒŋ 美音 ə'lɔːŋ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 向前：

The police told the crowd to move along.
警察叫人群向前移动。

  1. 高义频： 一道；一起：

along with
Would you like me to come along with you?
你愿意让我跟你一起去吗？

固定搭配

  • along with

  1. 与···一起

A sensible diet along with regular exercise is the best way to lose weight.
合理饮食和定期锻炼是减肥的最佳途径。

主语后跟有along with短语时，谓语动词的单复数应和along with前面的主语保持一致。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

Nowadays, cycling, along with jogging and swimming, __ (be) regarded as one of the best all-round forms of exercise.

答案 is

already adv

英音 ɔːl'redi 美音 ɔːl'redi

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 已经：

  • [表示在某个时间之前]：

We have already had a discussion over the plan.
我们已对这项计划进行了讨论。

  • [常用于句尾] [表示惊奇或意外]：

Is it 5 o’clock already?
已经5点了吗？

You can’t be hungry already — you had lunch only two hours ago!
你不会又饿了吧——你可是两小时前刚吃完午饭！

already一般用在肯定句中，在否定句和疑问句中多用yet。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

also多用于肯定句中，否定句中多用either。 also多用于书面语，口语中多用too或as well。

alternative n 重难点词汇

英音 ɔːl'tɜːnətɪv 美音 ɔːl'tɜːnətɪv

词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 2

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 选择；供选择的东西

alternative to
Minibuses with seats for 12 passengers offer an alternative to expensive taxis and crowded public transport.
相对于昂贵的出租车和拥挤的公共交通工具，12座的小公共汽车提供了另一种选择。

In pursuing a dream, we might focus on only one way of making it come true, forgetting that there may be alternatives.
追求梦想时，我们可能会只聚焦于实现梦想的一种方式，而忘记也许还有其他的选择。

固定搭配

  • have no alternative but to do sth

  1. 除了做某事别无选择：

I had no alternative but to report him to the police.
除了向警察举报他，我别无选择。

派生词汇

alternatively /ɔːl'tɜːrnətɪvli/ adv

or alternatively
I could come to your house, or alternatively we could meet in town.
我可以来你家找你，或者我们也可以在城里见面。

真题解析

[null]

alternative adj 重难点词汇

英音 ɔːl'tɜːnətɪv 美音 ɔːl'tɜːrnətɪv

词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 2

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [只用于名词前] 可供替代的；可供选择的
    that you can use, do, etc. instead of sth else：

alternative method
an alternative method of learning
其他的学习方法

The way was blocked, so we went by an alternative road.
这条路堵塞了，因此我们走了另一条路。

  1. 高义频： 非传统的；另类的
    different from what is usual or traditional ：

alternative lifestyle
an alternative lifestyle
另类的生活方式

固定搭配

  • alternative energy

  1. 替代能源 (指太阳能、风能、水能等)

派生词汇

alternatively /ɔːl'tɜːrnətɪvli/ adv

or alternatively
I could come to your house, or alternatively we could meet in town.
我可以来你家找你，或者我们也可以在城里见面。

真题解析

题目

The disappearance of dinosaurs is not necessarily caused by astronomical incidents. But___explanations are hard to find.
A.alternative
B.aggressive
C.ambiguous
D.apparent

答案 A
题目

As there is less and less coal and oil, scientists are exploring new ways of making use of ____(替代能源), such as sunlight, wind and water for power and fuel.

答案 alternative energy

 

although conj

英音 ɔːl'ðəʊ 美音 ɔːl'ðoʊ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [引导让步状语从句， 用法同though]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 尽管；虽然：

Although the job takes a signiﬁcant amount of time, most students agree that the experience is worth it.
尽管这份工作会花大量的时间，但是大部分学生都认为这个经历是值得的。

  1. 高义频： 然而；但是：

I don’t believe we’ve met before, although I must say you do look familiar.
我想我们以前没见过，不过我得说你看上去的确面熟。

although不与but连用，但可以与yet, still等表转折的副词连用。

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 完全地：

The train went slower and slower until it stopped altogether.
火车速度越来越慢，最后彻底停了下来。

always adv

英音 'ɔːlweɪz 美音 'ɔːlweɪz

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 总是；一直：

I'm always inspired by things of beauty and harmony.
我总是能从美好和谐的事物中受到启发。

Why are you always complaining about my cooking?
你为什么总抱怨我的厨艺？

always与进行时连用，有时表示因一件事情多次重复，说话人感觉焦躁或不满。

  1. 高义频： 永远：

Dear Mom, wherever I am, I will always love you.
亲爱的妈妈，无论我身在何处都永远爱您。

固定搭配

  • as always

  1. 同往常一样 (as usual)：

As always, he puts on his shoes and goes for a walk.
他和平时一样，穿上鞋出去散步了。

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 吃惊的；惊奇的(astonished)：

  • (be) amazed to do sth:

Mr Grant was amazed to ﬁnd 46 ancient gold coins inside the pot.
格兰特先生惊奇地发现罐子里有46枚古金币。

  • (be) amazed at / by:

I’m amazed at / by the progress you’ve made.
我对你取得的进步感到惊讶。

  • (be) amazed + (that) / how-从句：

I was amazed that he knew a lot about stamps.
我很惊讶他对邮票懂得很多。

amount n

英音 ə'maʊnt 美音 ə'maʊnt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [C] & [U] 数量；数额；总数：

large amounts of
When you are traveling, don’t display large amounts of cash to others.
旅行时，不要向他人显露大量的现金。

a huge amount of
A little bit of kindness will be rewarded with a huge amount of benefits.
滴水之恩当涌泉相报。

amounts of / a large (huge / small) amount of 尤与不可数名词连用。作主语时，谓语动词的单复数与amount的数保持一致。

Large amounts of money were spent on building the bridge.
大量的资金用在了这座桥的建造上。

There’s only a small amount of food.
只有一点儿食物。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

an art

英音 ən, æn 美音 ən

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [an一般用于以元音音素开始的词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (非特指的) 一 (个)：

a university
一所大学

an honest man
一个老实人

  1. 高义频： (一类事物中的) 任何一个 (any)：

A square has four sides.
正方形有四条边。

  1. 高义频： 一 (one)：

Rome was not built in a day.
罗马不是一天建成的。

  1. 高义频： 每一 (each)：

twenty dollars a week
每周20美元

three times a day
一日三次

  1. 高义频： 某一 (a certain，用于专有名词特别是人名前)：

Brian is gifted in writing music; he is very likely to be a Beethoven.
布莱恩有作曲天赋，他很有可能成为又一个贝多芬。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

Each of my cafes will have a different theme and an unique style.

答案 an → a
题目

As the kid, I loved to watch cartoons.

答案 the → a
题目

It takes them about a hour and a half to go to work every day.

答案 第一个a → an / one
题目

I can't tell you ____ way to the Wilsons' because we don’t have ____ Wilson here in the village.

答案 the; a
题目

The paper is due next month, and I am working seven days ____ week, often long into ____ night.

答案 a; the

and conj

英音 ənd 美音 ənd

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 和；又；而：

Drive slowly and carefully.
小心，慢点儿开车。(表示并列)

Come and give me a hand with this.
过来帮我一下。(表示目的)

He fell and cut his knee.
他跌倒了，划破了膝盖。(表示结果)

I’m feeling better and better.
我感觉越来越好。(表示程度)

He kept on talking and talking.
他不停地说啊说。(表示反复)

  1. 高义频： (只要…) 就：

Work hard and you’ll pass the exam.
只要用功，你就能通过考试。

Find ways to praise your children often, and you'll ﬁnd they will open their hearts to you.
想办法经常表扬你的孩子，你就会发现他们会对你敞开心扉。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

答案 or→and

答案 and
题目

The artist was born poor, ____ poor he remained all his life.
A.and
B.or
C.but
D.so

答案 A

announce vt

英音 ə'naʊns 美音 ə'naʊns

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 宣告；宣布：

Please remain seated; the winner of the prize will be announced soon.
请坐好，马上公布获奖者。

Mr White announced that he would go to China in February.
怀特先生宣布他将于二月份去中国。

  1. 高义频： (尤指在机场或火车站) 广播通知：

The pilot announced with apology that there would be a slight delay before setting down.
飞行员抱歉地通知，飞机会晚一点着陆。

  1. 低义频： 宣布…的到来 / 出席：

Would you announce the guests as they come in?
客人来时你通报一声好吗？

  • if anything

  1. [口语] [用于补充内容以强调前面所说的话] 要是有什么的话：

对于失败山姆看起来并不怎么失望，要是说有什么的话，倒是这事儿结束了，他好像松了一口气。

apart adv

英音 ə'pɑːt 美音 ə'pɑːrt

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 相隔地；相距地：

  1. 高义频： 分开地：

set,apart

他嗓音深沉，这使他不同于我们小镇上的其他人。

I can’t tell the twins apart.
我区分不开这对双胞胎。

  1. 高义频： 零散地；成碎片地：

taking apart
Rod loves taking apart clocks. However, he never manages to put them together again.
罗德喜欢把钟表拆开，但他从未能再组装上。

came apart
I’m sorry, the cup just came apart in my hands.
很抱歉，这个杯子竟在我手上碎了。

fell apart
His marriage fell apart.
他的婚姻破裂了。

  • apart from

  1. 高义频： 除…外 (别无)；若不：

  1. 高义频： 除…外 (尚有)：

Apart from providing warmth, what was fire used for?
除了用来取暖，火还有什么用处？

  • be worlds apart

  1. 完全不同；截然相反：

Their experience of life is worlds apart.
他们的生活经历完全不同。

我当时不在场，但据说音乐会很精彩。

appear vi 重难点词汇

英音 ə'pɪə(r) 美音 ə'pɪr

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 出现
    反义词 disappear:

One day a stranger appeared on my doorstep.
一天，一个陌生人出现在我家门前。

  1. 低义频： 参加演出；亮相：

She has already appeared in a few films.
她已参演过几部影片。

The principal appeared on television to advocate the reform.
校长上了电视节目，倡导改革。

  1. 高义频： 似乎；显得 (seem)：

  • appear (to be) + adj / n:

She tried hard to appear (to be) calm at the job interview.
求职面试时她努力让自己显得镇静。

He appeared to be a gentleman — he was wearing a suit, not like a thief at all.
他看起来像个正人君子——穿着西装，根本不像小偷。

  • appear to do sth:

There’s evidence that people who have a purpose in life appear to do better.
有证据显示，有生活目标的人似乎表现得更加出色。

  • it appears + (that) 从句：

It appeared that he had a taste for music.
他似乎喜欢音乐。

Things aren't always what they appear (to be).
事情往往不是它们看上去的样子。

  1. 低义频： 出版；刊登；发表：

His new book will be appearing in the spring.
他的新书将在春季出版。

辨析 appear, look, seem

三者都有“看起来”之意。

arrange v 重难点词汇

英音 ə'reɪndʒ 美音 ə'reɪndʒ

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 安排；筹划
    to make plans and preparations for sth to happen：

  • arrange (for sb / sth) to do sth:

Dave arranged for someone to drive him home.
戴夫安排人开车送他回家。

Nobel arranged in his will to give the largest part of his money to establish the Nobel prizes.
诺贝尔在遗嘱中把他的大部分钱捐献出来设立诺贝尔奖。

  • arrange (sth) with sb (about sth):

I’ve arranged with the neighbours about feeding the cat while we are away.
我们外出期间喂猫的事，我已和邻居安排妥了。

The headmaster arranged a meeting with all of the teachers.
校长安排了和所有老师开会。

  • arrange + wh- to do sth:

We haven't yet arranged when to meet.
我们还没定好何时见面。

  • arrange + that 从句：

The manager arranged that the meeting should be put off for a couple of days.
经理安排会议推迟几天。

In China, many parents arrange everything for their children and pave the way for their success.
在中国， 许多父母为孩子安排一切，为他们的成功铺路。

  1. 高义频： 排列；整理
    to put sth in a particular order：

The list is arranged alphabetically.
这个名单是按字母顺序排列的。

You can arrange things from beginning to end, small to large or by some other order.
你可以按照从头到尾、从小到大或别的顺序来整理物品。

  1. 低义频： 编写 / 改编 (乐曲)
    to write or change a piece of music：

write and arrange musical compositions
编写并改编音乐作品

固定搭配

  • arranged marriage

  1. 包办婚姻

the arrivals lounge
抵达大厅

We hope for the arrival of good news.
我们盼望着好消息的到来。

On,Upon arrival
On / Upon arrival, Jimmy found a long line of applicants waiting to be interviewed.
一到那里，吉米就发现申请者排起了长队等着面试。

  1. 高义频： [C] 到达者；到达物：

early / late / new arrivals
早到/晚到/新到者

真题解析

[null]

arrive vi

英音 ə'raɪv 美音 ə'raɪv

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 到达；送达；到来：

Christmas soon arrived.
圣诞节很快就到了。

A package arrived for you this morning.
今天上午你的一个包裹到了。

arrived in
We arrived in London in the morning.
我们上午到达了伦敦。

arrived at
They arrived at the station just in time.
他们及时赶到了车站。

arrive in指到达相对大的地方，arrive at指到达相对小的地点。

辨析 arrive, get, reach

三者均有“到达”之意。

固定搭配

  • arrive at

  1. 达成 (协议) (reach)；得出 (结论)：

arrive at an agreement / a decision
达成协议/作出决定

arrive at a conclusion
It took a long time to arrive at a conclusion.
花了很长时间才得出结论。

as conj

英音 əz 美音 əz

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 当…时候；一面…一面…；随着：

They sang songs as they were doing farm work.
他们一边干农活，一边唱着歌。

As the average age of the population increases, there are more and more old people to care for.
随着人口平均年龄的增长，有越来越多的老年人需要关照。

  1. 高义频： 因为；既然：

As he wasn’t ready in time, we went without him.
因为他没有及时准备好，我们没等他就走了。

辨析 because, since, as, for

  1. 高义频： 虽然；尽管：

Clever as she is, she works very hard. / Although she is clever, she works very hard.
尽管聪明，她还是很努力。

as意为“尽管”时，引导的从句要用倒装语序，其结构为：形容词 /名词 / 副词 / 动词原形 + as + 主语…。名词提前时，去掉冠词。

Child as he was, he knew a lot. / Although he was a child, he knew a lot.
他虽然是个孩子，但懂的很多。

  1. 高义频： 如；像；按照(like)：

When in Rome do as the Romans do.
入乡随俗。

We’d better leave things as they are until the police arrive.
在警察到来前，我们最好让现场保持原样。

表示比较或方式的as从句一般用正常语序，但是，在正式用语中，as从句有时也用倒装语序。

She looks forward, as does her secretary, to the completion of the building.
和她的秘书一样，她也盼望着大楼竣工。

固定搭配

  • as for

  1. 至于…；就…而言：

As for my favorite figure in Chinese history, it must be Wei Yuan, a great thinker in the late Qing Dynasty.
至于我最喜欢的中国历史人物，他一定是晚清伟大的思想家魏源。

  • as if / though

  1. 好像；似乎：

It looks as if it is going to rain.
看样子好像要下雨。

I remember the whole thing as if it happened yesterday.
整个事情我都记得很清楚，就像发生在昨天一样。

He speaks English perfectly as if / though he had lived in England for many years.
他英语讲得很好，好像他在英国生活了很多年似的。

as if / though常用于引导表语从句或状语从句，如果是不真实的情况，从句中常用过去时表示虚拟语气。

  • as it is / was

  1. [置于句首] 实际上；[置于句末] 已经：

As it is, I have a garden full of sweet-smelling roses for most of the year.
其实，我有一座花园，一年中大部分时间都玫瑰飘香。

I’ve already gone into debt as it is, so don’t expect any more money from me.
我已经欠债了，所以不要指望我会再出钱。

  • as to sth

  1. 关于某事：

I’m in a puzzle as to what to do next.
关于下一步该做什么我也不知道。

[null]

题目

题目

题目

题目

题目

— Coach, can I continue with the training?

— Sorry, you can’t ____ you haven’t recovered from the knee injury.
A.until
B.before

D.unless

as adv

英音 əz 美音 əz

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 同样地：

Ten years ago the population of our village was twice as large as that of theirs.
十年前我们村子的人口数量是他们的两倍。

Some scientists even say we can live as long as 130 years!
一些科学家甚至说我们能活到130岁！

否定句中也可用so代替as。

A friend is not so soon gotten as lost.
交友慢，失友快。

Maybe things are not as / so bad as they seem to be.
也许事情并不像看上去那么糟。

  1. 高义频： (正) 如…一样：

  • 作关系代词，引导限制性定语从句，常与 such和the same连用：

He is not such a fool as he looks.
他并不像看起来那么傻。

我收到的T恤和网上展示的不一样。

  • 作关系代词，引导非限制性定语从句，从句可位于主句前、中、后：

As we all know, success comes from hard work.
众所周知，成功源于勤奋。

ask v

英音 ɑːsk 美音 æsk

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 问；询问：

She asked Mary what time it was.
她问玛丽几点了。

We’ll have to ask someone the way to the station.
我们得去问一下车站怎么走。

asked about
She asked about Jesse’s health.
她询问了杰西的健康状况。

  1. 高义频： 要求；请求：

  • ask (sb) to do sth:

One evening, a passer-by asked to stay for the night.
一天晚上，有个过路人请求借宿一晚。

People may feel forced when asked to do things that they don’t want to.
当被要求做自己不愿做的事情时，人们会有种被迫的感觉。

  • ask + that / wh- 从句:

She asked that she should be kept informed of developments.
她要求向她报告进展情况。

  • ask (sb) for sth:

Don’t be afraid of asking (others) for help when it is needed.
需要时不要害怕(向他人)求助。

I went into a cafe and asked for a coffee.
我走进一家咖啡馆要了杯咖啡。

  1. 高义频： 邀请：

  • ask sb to do sth:

She’s asked him to come to the party.
她已邀请他来参加聚会。

  1. 高义频： 索要 (价格)：

asking,for
He’s asking ￡80 a month rent for that flat.
那套公寓月租他要价80英镑。

固定搭配

  • ask for trouble

  1. 自找麻烦；自讨苦吃

We’re looking for people who would be willing to assist in / with the group’s work.
我们正在寻找愿意帮助该小组工作的人。

assisted,in
I swam to Dad quickly and assisted him in climbing / to climb onto the boat.
我迅速游向父亲，并协助他爬到船上。

辨析 assist, help, aid

三者都有“帮助”之意，但侧重点有所不同。

  1. 高义频： 假定；设想
    to accept or think that sth is true although you have no proof：

It is generally assumed (that) stress is caused by too much work.
普遍认为，压力系工作过重所致。

be assumed that
Where unemployment and crime are high, it can be assumed that the latter is due to the former.
在失业率和犯罪率高的地方，我们可以假定高犯罪率是由高失业率造成的。

attend v 重难点词汇

英音 ə'tend 美音 ə'tend

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [正式用语]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 出席；参加：

attend a lecture / party / meeting / an interview
听课/参加聚会/参加会议/参加面试

Please let us know if you are unable to attend.
如果不能出席请通知我们。

辨析 join, join in, take part in, attend

四者都常译为“参加”。

  1. 高义频： 上 (学)：

That holiday morning I didn’t have to attend school.
那个假日的早上，我不必去上学。

  1. 低义频： 看护；照料：

The patient was attended by a nurse.
病人由一名护士照料。

固定搭配

  • attend to

  1. 照料；处理；接待 (serve)：

Nurses are busy attending to the wounded.
护士正忙着照顾伤员。

— Would you like to join us in the game?
你想和我们一起做游戏吗？

— I’m afraid not, for I have something important to attend to.
恐怕不行，我有重要的事要处理。

Excuse me, sir. Are you being attended to?
先生，打扰下。有人接待你吗？

派生词汇

attendance /ə'tendəns/ n [U] & [C] attendant /ə'tendənt/ n [C]

真题解析

题目

We will ____ (参加) a meeting to celebrate the sixtieth birthday of the P.R. China.

答案 attend

 

attention n

英音 ə'tenʃn 美音 ə'tenʃn

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 注意；专心：

have your attention
May / Could I have your attention, please?
请注意!

turned,attention,to
He turned his attention back to the road again.
他把注意力又转回到道路上。

  1. 高义频： 兴趣；关注：

The post has since gained the attention of social media users all over the world.
之后，这个帖子得到了世界各地社交媒体用户的关注。

the centre of attention
Rob loves being the centre of attention.
罗布喜欢成为人们关注的焦点。

  1. 高义频： 关心；照料：

Thank you for your kind attention.
谢谢你善意的关心。

  1. 低义频： 维修；保养：

needs,attention
The old car needs a lot of attention.
这辆旧车该大修了。

  1. 低义频： 立正姿势：

Attention
Attention!
立正！

standing at attention
They are standing at attention.
他们在立正站着。

固定搭配

  • attract / catch / get the attention of …

  1. 吸引 / 引起 / 得到……的注意：

She waved to attract the attention of the waitress.
她挥手想引起服务员的注意。

The excellent football player quickly caught the attention of the public.
这个出色的足球运动员很快就吸引了公众的注意。

  • bring sth to sb’s attention

  1. 使某事引起某人的 注意：

Why don't you bring it to his attention that you're too ill to work on?
你为什么不告诉他你病得很厉害，不能继续工作呢？

  • call / draw attention to

  1. 使人们关注：

The purpose of the campaign is to draw public attention to the needs of the tall.
这项活动的目的是让公众关注高个子人群的需求。

  • hold / keep sb’s attention

  1. 保持某人的注意力：

This game is fun and is sure to keep children's attention.
这个游戏很有趣，一定能保持孩子们的注意力。

  • pay attention to

  1. 注意：

On the bus, you will often notice someone paying more attention to his mobile phone.
在公共汽车上，你常会看到有人更专注于看自己的手机。

  • with attention

  1. 专心致志地：

The lawyer listened with full attention, trying not to miss any point.
这位律师全神贯注地听着，竭力不漏掉任何要点。

[null]

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 观众；听众：

an audience of
When Mozart’s music was performed in America, there was an audience of 100,000 people.
在美国演奏莫扎特的乐曲时，台下有10万观众。

The lecture drew a large audience.
这个讲座吸引了很多听众。

audience是集体名词，作主语时，如果作为整体看待，谓语动词用单数；如果强调各个成员，谓语动词用复数。

The audience was large.
观众很多。

The audience are dressed in a variety of ways.
观众的穿着各不相同。

    the official right or permission to do sth：

available adj 重难点词汇

英音 ə'veɪləbl 美音 ə'veɪləbl

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 可用的；可得到的
    able to be used or can easily be bought or found：

Cold drinks will be available at the Sports Center.
体育中心有冷饮供应。

With all the information available, they found the hotel in the mountain easily.
所有信息在手，他们很容易就找到了山里的旅馆。

available to
In the 1940s, electricity was available to people in almost all areas of the United States.
20世纪40年代，几乎美国所有地区的人都用上了电。

available for
There will be four basketball courts available for our use with one teacher watching over each game.
将有四个篮球场供我们使用，每场比赛都有一名教师监视。

  1. 高义频： (人) 有空的
    (of a person) free to be seen, talked to, etc.：

I would have gone to my cousin’s birthday party last night, but I was not available.
昨天晚上我本想去参加堂兄的生日聚会，但我没空。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

availability /əˌveɪlə'bɪləti/ n [U]

答案 available / free
题目

— Can you lend me the book Gone with the Wind?

— Sorry. I returned it to the library just now. Maybe it is still ____(可借到的).

答案 available

average n 重难点词汇

英音 'ævərɪdʒ 美音 'ævərɪdʒ

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C] & [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 平均；平均数：

The average of 3, 8 and 10 is 7.
数字3、8、10的平均数是7。

an average of
I spend an average of about $200 a year on books.
我平均每年大约花200美元买书。

  1. 高义频： 一般水平；平均标准：

below / above,average
below / above average
低于/超过平均水平

the national average
the national average
全国平均水平

固定搭配

  • on average

  1. 平均；一般地：

On average we have five classes a day.
我们平均每天上五节课。

Women, on average, live longer.
女性一般更长寿。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

He was a good student and scored__ (高于平均水平) in most subjects.

答案 above average
题目

Last year the number of students who graduated with a driving license reached 200,000, ____ average of 40,000 per year.

答案 an
题目

On ____ (平均), people who don’t smoke are healthier than people who do.

答案 average

 

average adj 重难点词汇

英音 'ævərɪdʒ 美音 'ævərɪdʒ

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [无比较级]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [只用于名词前] 平均的：

Scientists believe the world’s average temperature has risen by about 0.8℃ since 1900.
科学家认为自1900年以来，世界平均温度已经升高了约0.8℃。

The average number of electronic devices rose from four per household in 1992 to 13 in 2007.
平均每户家庭的电子设备数量从1992年的4件上升到了2007年的13件。

  1. 高义频： 中等的；适中的
    normal or typical：

of average intelligence
children of average intelligence
智力一般的儿童

of average height
He was in his late twenties and of average height.
他年近三十，中等个头。

  1. 低义频： 平常的；普遍的
    not special; ordinary：

Freddy was an average student, but not an average person.
弗雷迪是一名普通的学生，但却不是一个普通的人。

avoid vt 重难点词汇

英音 ə'vɔɪd 美音 ə'vɔɪd

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 避免；防止
    to prevent sth bad from happening：

  • avoid doing sth:

To avoid missing the last train, please check the last train times posted in stations.
为了避免错过末班列车，请查阅车站张贴的末班列车时刻表。

Road safety is taught to young children to avoid road accident.
儿童需要学习道路安全知识，以避免交通事故。

  1. 高义频： 回避；避开
    to stay away from sb or sth, or to deliberately not do sth：

  • avoid doing sth:

Neighbors should do all they can to avoid disturbing other people.
邻居应尽量避免打扰他人。

Generally we dislike arguments, and we avoid topics which lead to disagreement.
我们通常不喜欢争吵，会回避引起争执的话题。

avoid不接不定式作宾语。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

I quickly lower myself, ducking my head to avoid_____(look) directly into his eyes.

答案 looking

词频 3 | 口语 1 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [不用于名词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 醒着的：
    反义词 asleep

wide awake
Light from street lamps is leading to birds being wide awake when they should be asleep.
路灯的光使鸟在该睡着的时候还完全醒着。

keep,awake
A cup of coffee will keep me awake all night.
只喝一杯咖啡就会使我整晚睡不着。

词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 奖；奖金；奖品；奖状：

an award of $10,000
10000美元的奖金

win,get,receive an award
win / get / gain / obtain / receive an award
获奖

present awards
颁奖

"Lifetime Achievement" award
终身成就奖

award for
The award for this year's best actress went to Emma Stone.
本年度最佳女演员的得奖者是艾玛·斯通。

辨析 reward, award, prize

aware adj 重难点词汇

英音 ə'weə(r) 美音 ə'wer

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 1

用法点拨 [不用于名词前]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 意识到的；察觉到的：

  • (be) aware of:

People around the world should be aware of the real situation of water shortage.
全世界人民都应该意识到水资源短缺的真实情况。

They suddenly became aware of people looking at them.
他们突然发觉有人在看着他们。

  • (be) aware + that 从句:

If she had been aware that the mushrooms were poisonous, she would not have picked them for dinner.
要是知道这些蘑菇有毒，她就不会采来做晚餐了。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

away adv

英音 ə'weɪ 美音 ə'weɪ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 离；离开；间隔：

Go / Run away!
走/跑开！

away from
His speech is away from the subject.
他的讲话离题了。

away from
The sea is only two miles away from here.
大海离这儿只有两英里。

The sports meet is two weeks away.
离运动会还有两个星期。

  1. 高义频： 朝另一个方向：

Don’t look away while driving.
开车时不要四处张望。

  1. 高义频： 在别处；在适当的地方：

He put his tools away.
他把工具收起来了。

  1. 高义频： 不在；外出：

He is away in town.
他去城里了。

  1. 低义频： [多与动词连用] ...去；...掉：

wash away
冲走；冲掉

The snow melted away.
雪融化了。

awesome adj

英音 'ɔːsəm 美音 'ɔːsəm

词频 1 | 口语 0 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 低义频： 引起敬畏的；可怕的：
    very impressive or very difﬁcult and perhaps rather frightening：

They had an awesome task ahead.
前面有十分艰巨的任务等着他们。

  1. 高义频： [尤用于美语，非正式用语] 极好的；了不起的：

There is only one word to describe the best player in the world — awesome!
只有一个词能够形容这位世界上最好的球员——了不起！

awful adj

英音 'ɔːfl 美音 'ɔːfl

词频 3 | 口语 3 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [非正式用语] 糟糕的；恶劣的；讨厌的 (terrible)：

What awful weather!
天气糟糕透了!

You can certainly borrow my notes if you don’t mind my awful handwriting.
如果你不介意我糟糕的字迹，当然可以借我的笔记。

  1. 高义频： [非正式用语] [只用于名词前] 非常的；很多的：

It’s going to cost an awful lot of money.
这要花很多的钱。

I’ve got an awful headache.
我头疼得要命。

  1. 高义频： 可怕的；骇人听闻的 (terrible)

固定搭配

  • look / feel awful

  1. 面带病容；很不舒服
    (look / feel ill)：

2012 重庆
You look awful. Do you have a cold?
你气色很不好，感冒了吗？

awkward adj

英音 'ɔːkwəd 美音 'ɔːkwərd

词频 2 | 口语 1 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 尴尬的；别扭的
    embarrasing：

awkward silence
an awkward silence
令人尴尬的沉默

I felt awkward, so I smiled at him.
我感到很尴尬，冲他笑了笑。

  1. 高义频： 使用不便的；难以应付的(difficult)：

an awkward machine
不好用的机器

ask an awkward question
问一个难以回答的问题

  1. 高义频： 不方便的 (inconvenient)：

Please arrange the next meeting at a less awkward time.
请把下次会议时间安排得方便些。
